     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Batman:_Arkham">
       <i>
        Batman: Arkham
       </i>
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Harley_Quinn&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Batman: Arkham">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Arkham_Knight_Harley_Quinn_Promo.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="463" data-file-width="430" height="237" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/d/d3/Arkham_Knight_Harley_Quinn_Promo.jpg/220px-Arkham_Knight_Harley_Quinn_Promo.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/d/d3/Arkham_Knight_Harley_Quinn_Promo.jpg/330px-Arkham_Knight_Harley_Quinn_Promo.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/d/d3/Arkham_Knight_Harley_Quinn_Promo.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Arkham_Knight_Harley_Quinn_Promo.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Harley Quinn in a promotional image for
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Batman:_Arkham_Knight" title="Batman: Arkham Knight">
          Batman: Arkham Knight
         </a>
        </i>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Arleen_Sorkin" title="Arleen Sorkin">
        Arleen Sorkin
       </a>
       reprises her role of Harley Quinn in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Batman:_Arkham_Asylum" title="Batman: Arkham Asylum">
         Batman: Arkham Asylum
        </a>
       </i>
       , as the secondary antagonist of the game, here with a new costume based on a nurse uniform. She takes control of Arkham, allowing Joker to escape, releases
       <a href="/wiki/Poison_Ivy_(comics)" title="Poison Ivy (comics)">
        Poison Ivy
       </a>
       from her cell, and kidnaps Warden
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quincy_Sharp" title="Quincy Sharp">
        Quincy Sharp
       </a>
       . After Batman rescues Sharp, he confronts her and locks her in a cell. She returns in the
       <a href="/wiki/Scarecrow_(DC_Comics)" title="Scarecrow (DC Comics)">
        Scarecrow's
       </a>
       final nightmare as one of the guards escorting Batman away. To date this was the last time Arleen Sorkin voiced her iconic character.
      </li>
      <li>
       Harley Quinn appears in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Batman:_Arkham_City" title="Batman: Arkham City">
         Batman: Arkham City
        </a>
       </i>
       , voiced by
       <a href="/wiki/Tara_Strong" title="Tara Strong">
        Tara Strong
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">
        <a href="#cite_note-42">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         42
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       She is shown wearing a biker-girl themed costume in this game, using a low-key version of her usual makeup, with heavy eyeshadow in lieu of her domino mask. This costume featured knee high wedge boots and a corset like top. She wears her hair in two pigtails on both sides of her head, which she has dip dyed red and black. She now has tattoos of the Joker on her upper right arm and on the left side of her waist. She is characterized as being dangerously unstable and incompetent; at one point early in the game, she may be overheard having a conversation that inadvertently reveals key details of the Joker's plans. She is alternately loathed and lusted after by the Joker's gang, whom she treats as a group of dim-witted thugs. Harley had captured some doctors and police officers as hostages when Batman finds her in the church. Harley manages to get away while the Joker's henchmen fight Batman who ends up defeating them and saving the hostages (only for them to be later captured by the
       <a href="/wiki/Riddler" title="Riddler">
        Riddler
       </a>
       ). Batman later encounters Harley in the Sionis Steel Mill where she was with the Joker. She later steals the cure for the Joker's illness while Batman was fighting Mr. Freeze for it, but is bound and gagged by
       <a href="/wiki/Talia_al_Ghul" title="Talia al Ghul">
        Talia al Ghul
       </a>
       . When the Joker dies from his illness following Batman's fight with Clayface (who was masquerading as a healthier Joker), Quinn was with the Joker's henchmen when Batman brought his dead body out of the theater. After completing the game, the player can enter the Joker's office, where several negative pregnancy tests and a positive test can be found, hinting she may be pregnant with the Joker's child. In the ending credits of the new game plus mode, Harley is heard singing a version of the lullaby "Hush, Little Baby," promising that "Mama's gonna kill for you the whole damn world." Harley appears in "Harley Quinn's Revenge" expansion as the main antagonist, seeking revenge on Batman for the death of the Joker; her doctor noted Harley was "losing it big time" because the Joker was the only thing keeping Harley relatively sane. By this time, Harley has dyed her hair completely black and wears almost all black, with a "J" necklace and mourning veil. After escaping from a temporary holding area following the destruction of Arkham City, Harley transforms the Steel Mill (the Joker's former base of operations) into a gigantic memorial of him. She is later beaten by the duo of Batman and Robin and taken into custody by the GCPD. Included as an
       <a href="/wiki/Easter_egg" title="Easter egg">
        easter egg
       </a>
       in the manager's office of the Steel Mill, there is a crib with
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Scarface_(comics)" title="Scarface (comics)">
        Scarface
       </a>
       painted as the Joker inside, surrounded by dozens of negative pregnancy tests accompanied by a single positive pregnancy test, which indicates that she had a miscarriage, the positive test was false, or after several failed attempts she finally got pregnant just before the Joker died.
      </li>
      <li>
       Harley Quinn introduced Martin Tremblay, president of Warner Brothers Interactive Entertainment, at the
       <a href="/wiki/Nintendo" title="Nintendo">
        Nintendo
       </a>
       Press Conference at E3 2012 where Batman Arkham City: Armored Edition was introduced for the
       <a href="/wiki/Wii_U" title="Wii U">
        Wii U
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       Harley Quinn appears in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Batman:_Arkham_City_Lockdown" title="Batman: Arkham City Lockdown">
         Batman: Arkham City Lockdown
        </a>
       </i>
       , where she kidnaps a reporter to use as a hostage to free the Joker. After luring Batman into a trap, she tries to execute the bound and gagged reporter, but is stopped by one of Batman's batarangs. She is once again voiced by Tara Strong.
      </li>
      <li>
       Dr. Harleen Quinzel, M.D. appears briefly in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Batman:_Arkham_Origins" title="Batman: Arkham Origins">
         Batman: Arkham Origins
        </a>
       </i>
       before her transformation into Harley Quinn. She interviews Joker at Blackgate Prison and falls in love with him after he confesses his fascination with someone who he considers special to him (Batman). She is voiced again by Tara Strong.
      </li>
      <li>
       While Dr. Harleen Quinzel, M.D. never makes a physical appearance in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Batman:_Arkham_Origins_Blackgate" title="Batman: Arkham Origins Blackgate">
         Batman: Arkham Origins Blackgate
        </a>
       </i>
       , she is referred to in the unlockable Detective Case titled "Doctor's Orders." According to the Detective Case, Quinzel's increasing obsession with the Joker is not going unnoticed by her fellow staff, who are beginning to worry that the Joker may be manipulating Quinzel. The Case also states that Quinzel has started referring to the Joker as "Mister J" in her personal journal with hearts drawn around his name, rather than "Patient ARK119805."
      </li>
      <li>
       Harley Quinn appears in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Batman:_Arkham_Knight" title="Batman: Arkham Knight">
         Batman: Arkham Knight
        </a>
       </i>
       , voiced again by Tara Strong.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2014MarCVG_43-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-2014MarCVG-43">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         43
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       In the main story, it's revealed that in between the events of Arkham City and the current game, she's become a very competent gang leader, having recovered control of the Joker's former gang (including the members that were plotting to overthrow her or desert her) and has even become one of Gotham's main gang leaders, recruited by Scarecrow in his plan to kill Batman. She tries to break free and recruit the victims of Joker's blood transfusion who were not affected by the cure, all of whom started to display traces of his appearance and behavior, but they all end up dead after she was betrayed by one of the Joker patients that was working for her.
       <ul>
        <li>
         Apart from the main game, she is a playable character via pre-order downloadable content in a story-driven mission, featuring her own weapons and abilities; the content also includes four challenge maps for the character. In her mission, which takes place shortly before the main story, Harley breaks into the
         <a href="/wiki/Bl%C3%BCdhaven" title="Bldhaven">
          Bldhaven
         </a>
         prison to free Poison Ivy, defeating all police officers and, with Ivy's help, Nightwing.
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HarleyDLC_44-0">
          <a href="#cite_note-HarleyDLC-44">
           <span>
            [
           </span>
           44
           <span>
            ]
           </span>
          </a>
         </sup>
        </li>
       </ul>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Injustice:_Gods_Among_Us">
       <i>
        Injustice: Gods Among Us
       </i>
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Harley_Quinn&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Injustice: Gods Among Us">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <ul>
      <li>
       Harley Quinn appears as a playable fighter in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Injustice:_Gods_Among_Us" title="Injustice: Gods Among Us">
         Injustice: Gods Among Us
        </a>
       </i>
       voiced again by Tara Strong.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">
        <a href="#cite_note-45">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         45
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       In the alternate universe depicted in the game, Quinn establishes the Joker Clan to honor the Clown Prince after he is murdered by Superman. She is part of Batman's Insurgency, and reacts very negatively when the "Prime" Joker appears, believing him to be a fake. The Joker still temporarily gains her trust after proving himself to be the real deal, but she gets over it again once he threatens to kill her when she fails to defeat her Earth's version of Lex Luthor who, unknown to them both at the time, is a fellow Insurgent posing as an ally of Superman. In her battle ending, she had gone to marry The Joker, but after he playfully smashed her face into a cake, years of abuse made Harley snap. Using the ceremonial knife she slit The Joker's throat, killing him. It is then stated she permanently became a patient at the Arkham Asylum, still wearing her wedding gown. That happens not in our universe but where everyone is at ends with each other.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">
        <a href="#cite_note-46">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         46
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Lego_Batman">
       <i>
        Lego Batman
       </i>
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Harley_Quinn&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Lego Batman">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <ul>
      <li>
       She appears in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Lego_Batman:_The_Videogame" title="Lego Batman: The Videogame">
         Lego Batman: The Videogame
        </a>
       </i>
       , with her sound effects provided by
       <a href="/wiki/Grey_DeLisle" title="Grey DeLisle">
        Grey DeLisle
       </a>
       . She appears as an enemy of Batman and a 1st deputy of the Joker.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">
        <a href="#cite_note-47">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         47
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">
        <a href="#cite_note-48">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         48
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       Harley Quinn in Lego Batman is a playable character and can be unlocked through the villain levels, and carries a pistol and her giant mallet. She can perform high jumps like most women in the game.
      </li>
      <li>
       Harley Quinn appears as a minor antagonist in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Lego_Batman_2:_DC_Super_Heroes" title="Lego Batman 2: DC Super Heroes">
         Lego Batman 2: DC Super Heroes
        </a>
       </i>
       , voiced by
       <a href="/wiki/Laura_Bailey_(voice_actress)" title="Laura Bailey (voice actress)">
        Laura Bailey
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">
        <a href="#cite_note-49">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         49
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       Harley Quinn appears as a playable character in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Lego_Batman_3:_Beyond_Gotham" title="Lego Batman 3: Beyond Gotham">
         Lego Batman 3: Beyond Gotham
        </a>
       </i>
       , with
       <a href="/wiki/Tara_Strong" title="Tara Strong">
        Tara Strong
       </a>
       reprising her role.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Cultural_impact">
       Cultural impact
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Harley_Quinn&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Cultural impact">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Filmmaker and comic book fan
      <a href="/wiki/Kevin_Smith" title="Kevin Smith">
       Kevin Smith
      </a>
      named
      <a href="/wiki/Harley_Quinn_Smith" title="Harley Quinn Smith">
       his daughter
      </a>
      after Harley Quinn; she made a cameo appearance in
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Jay_and_Silent_Bob_Strike_Back" title="Jay and Silent Bob Strike Back">
        Jay and Silent Bob Strike Back
       </a>
      </i>
      as an infant Silent Bob in the opening scene, and was recently featured in his reality television show
      <a href="/wiki/Comic_Book_Men" title="Comic Book Men">
       Comic Book Men
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">
       <a href="#cite_note-50">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        50
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      She will appear alongside
      <a href="/wiki/Johnny_Depp" title="Johnny Depp">
       Johnny Depp
      </a>
      's daughter
      <a href="/wiki/Lily-Rose_Depp" title="Lily-Rose Depp">
       Lily-Rose Depp
      </a>
      in the 2015
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Comedy_horror" title="Comedy horror">
       comedy horror
      </a>
      film
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Yoga_Hosers" title="Yoga Hosers">
        Yoga Hosers
       </a>
      </i>
      .
     </p>
